  Variable legend: `u` is the wave profile; `U_line` is the contraction-compatible update.

### Hacking Theory

- `P.1`
  Equation:

  \[\pi_{\mathrm{P_1}}^+ = \pi_{\mathrm{P_1}}^- \oplus e_{\mathrm{P_1}}, \qquad e_{\mathrm{P_1}} \in E_{\mathrm{safe}} \iff \mathrm{seal}(e_{\mathrm{P_1}})=1 \land \mathrm{budget}(e_{\mathrm{P_1}})\le B_{\mathrm{P_1}}\]

  Variable legend: `pi` is the route, `e_line` the next admissible edge, `B_line` the seal budget.
  Reading: essence load / fluid carriage / volatile heat line.
  Confidence: mixed

- `P.10`
  Equation:

  \[\pi_{\mathrm{P_10}}^+ = \pi_{\mathrm{P_10}}^- \oplus e_{\mathrm{P_10}}, \qquad e_{\mathrm{P_10}} \in E_{\mathrm{safe}} \iff \mathrm{seal}(e_{\mathrm{P_10}})=1 \land \mathrm{budget}(e_{\mathrm{P_10}})\le B_{\mathrm{P_10}}\]

  Variable legend: `pi` is the route, `e_line` the next admissible edge, `B_line` the seal budget.
  Reading: verification checkpoint / cycle completion / essence load line.
  Confidence: mixed

- `P.11`
  Equation:

  \[\pi_{\mathrm{P_11}}^+ = \pi_{\mathrm{P_11}}^- \oplus e_{\mathrm{P_11}}, \qquad e_{\mathrm{P_11}} \in E_{\mathrm{safe}} \iff \mathrm{seal}(e_{\mathrm{P_11}})=1 \land \mathrm{budget}(e_{\mathrm{P_11}})\le B_{\mathrm{P_11}}\]

  Variable legend: `pi` is the route, `e_line` the next admissible edge, `B_line` the seal budget.

### Game Theory

- `P.1`
  Equation:

  \[y_{\mathrm{P_1}}^+ = \operatorname*{argmin}_{y \in \Delta(\mathcal{A})}\{R_{\mathrm{P_1}}(y) + \lambda_{\mathrm{P_1}} C(y, y_{\mathrm{P_1}}^-)\}\]

  Variable legend: `y` is the strategy distribution; `R_line` is risk and `C` the control-cost.
  Reading: essence load / fluid carriage / volatile heat line.
  Confidence: mixed

- `P.10`
  Equation:

  \[y_{\mathrm{P_10}}^+ = \operatorname*{argmin}_{y \in \Delta(\mathcal{A})}\{R_{\mathrm{P_10}}(y) + \lambda_{\mathrm{P_10}} C(y, y_{\mathrm{P_10}}^-)\}\]

## Direct Operational Meaning

This page is a STAR-MARKED RECIPE - a pharmaceutical formula where marginal stars serve as PROGRESS MARKERS. Each star corresponds to a stage of the recipe, and the star's visual properties (solid, hollow, red-dotted) encode what TYPE of operation occurs at that stage. Think of the stars as a...

Across the formal lenses, `f112v` behaves as a `star formulary` with 13 retort/transmutation events and 121 completion markers distributed across 47 visible lines.

### Folio Theorem

\[\rho_* = (\Psi_{\mathrm{final}} \circ \Psi_{\mathrm{body}} \circ \Psi_{\mathrm{entry}})(\rho_0)\]

The formal theorem of `f112v` is:

1. it belongs to `Star-Based Formulary` and executes `crystallization and product formation`
2. it carries `13` retort/transmutation signals, `115` circulation or extraction signals, and `121` completion markers across `47` visible lines
3. it preserves `20` union signals and `13` salt signals as the local closure budget
4. it contributes one station to the Pharmaceutical Part 1 crystal and the Book V training arc
